  \n                        <div class=\"card-lead\">\n                            <p></p><div><p>HUNTINGTON - It was 47 years ago on April 22, 1970, that the first Earth Day activated 20 million Americans from all walks of life and helped launch the modern environmental movement, which led to the passage of the landmark Clean Air Act, Clean Water Act, Endangered Species Act and many other groundbreaking environmental laws.</p></div><p></p>\n                        </div>\n                        \n                    \n                    \n                    <style>\n    </div>\n                    \n                    \n                        \n                        \n                        <div class=\"card-lead\">\n                            <p>HUNTINGTON - About 150 employers from the public and private sectors will be hoping to connect with job seekers Friday at the Big Sandy Superstore Arena during a job and resource fair hosted by U.S. Sen. Joe Manchin D-W.Va., Marshall University and a number of local organizations.</p>\n                        </div>\n                        \n                    \n                    \n
